<name>Diane Ko<//name><pictures>None< /pictures><time>1615407188163</time><review>This is our go to poke place, and it's nice that it's closeish to home. The staff is nice, and the fish is usually pretty fresh. I also really appreciate the option of spicy tuna as the base protein, since most places only offer "crab", and I'm not a fan of that.

Ordering during covid is pretty similar to ordering before covid. You walk in and go through the different steps (base, proteins, sauces, toppings).

Getting there can be a little tricky if you don't know what you're looking for. I find that the most convenient way to get there from Winton is to turn right at the Chase (before the stop sign) and then turn left on the first parking area you can turn left at. I usually park in that area and then walk over, as there's very limited parking by the front unless you need handicap parking.

Definitely recommend for poke if you're looking for a poke fix! It's not the same as true Hawaiian poke, but nothing I've had in the bay area is.<//review><resp>None</resp>< Rating>

< Review>
After years of numerous consultations with high profile dentists in southern California to highly regarded dentists in my hometown of Fresno I decided to have a consultation with Dr. Parker in Madera in 2013.  I was greeted by the nicest and most professional medical staff I had ever experienced.  If anyone knows me they know that unfortunately I have seen many medical offices in my past 15 years.  Dr. Parker sat down with me and reviewed my case.  It was the first time in the years I sought help a dentist had a clear understanding of my dental problems and a clear plan to achieve great results.  He was humble yet confident and I was immediately ready to entrust, invest and become a patient of Dr. Parker's in late 2013.  I needed significant reconstruction and restoration of my bite and smile.  My situation was complicated and involved special techniques and skills.  Most dentists I met with prior had plans that would have destroyed many of my healthy teeth to obtain the results needed to correct my bite and enhance my smile.  Dr. Parker's first statement to me was that he was a preservationist.  He wanted to save and protect every tooth possible in my mouth and he did!  Today my bite is better than it has ever been and my smile looks as though I was born with a perfect smile.  It looks totally natural and I feel so good about it!  A heavy weight has been lifted from my life thanks to Dr. Parker and his wonderful staff.  I'm forever grateful!  Since my experience one by one many of my family and friends are joining the Parker Dental family.  God Bless you and your staff.< /Review>

<Review>I so so much wanted to love this place. My sister has, for the first time, all her sisters plus mum here in LA, and we came with the most positive feelings and pumped up with love.

We loved the evening's concept and Doug's performance - highly recommended. However, the service was far from being acceptable - so server Marco ended up with zero tip‚Äã, a first for me in months. Unattentive and uncaring, serving ‚Äãmy cappuccino‚Äã in a way my saucer was like a soup. I could not lift the cup without spoiling me or the table. No sorry, no "let me get you a paper napkin" - just ignorant. We were a party of six. Three got their food - and politely waited for the others to receive their food - which came 15 mins later. We asked those who had their food to start eating. Marco cleared their plates before the last one had his food.

Sadly, my lobster pasta was totally inedible‚Äã. I had three of the six people on the table tasting it - they all agreed, the pasta tasted like as if it was warmed up in a microwave for the umpteenth time - and the temperature ‚Äãmade me really believe it was. I sort of feel bad making such an accusation, but we all felt like this. The mushroom risotto was delicious‚Äã, though.

I must admit: I broke my own golden rule: Never, I repeat never, order a lobster dish when there is no fresh lobster on the menu. If you do, you risk getting crap (not crab). I did.

I did not eat it. Nothing of it. No "was everything alright" - Marco took my plate without comment and served the food boxed to me. I politely declined. No response from Marco, who, by the way, did not even refill our glasses from the bottle of wine we had.

I don't know why this place doesn't get as much attention as it deserves. Guess that makes it a little known secret!

A really nice, quaint, and classic Italian restaurant on Colorado. I've been here two times and both times were worth it. The basketball court is the other end of the park where the playground and restrooms are. Two parkings, one Right next to the swimming pool and the other in front of the playground.
